<span id="freeTextContainer17584438441007827678">The movie was a lot better. I hardly recognised anything in this book, it was just so different. Different in a bad way too. Everything about this story made me sad. <br/><br/>Jack was born in Edinburgh, 1874, and with a frozen heart. His mother leaves him and the midwife, Madeleine gives him a cuckoo clock heart so that he can live. He remains there with the woman and she becomes his mother. Madeleine tells Jack three rules, so that he can continue to live with his odd little heart. "FIRSTLY: don’t touch</span>
  <span id="freeText17584438441007827678" style="display:none">The movie was a lot better. I hardly recognised anything in this book, it was just so different. Different in a bad way too. Everything about this story made me sad. <br /><br />Jack was born in Edinburgh, 1874, and with a frozen heart. His mother leaves him and the midwife, Madeleine gives him a cuckoo clock heart so that he can live. He remains there with the woman and she becomes his mother. Madeleine tells Jack three rules, so that he can continue to live with his odd little heart. "FIRSTLY: don’t touch the hands of your cuckoo-clock heart. SECONDLY: master your anger. THIRDLY: never, ever fall in love. For if you do, the hour hand will poke through your skin, your bones will shatter, and your heart will break once more." However, Jack soon breaks the third rule, and falls in love with a little singer girl. He's 10 at the time. In order to see her again, he goes to her school, only to find out that she's moved away. Instead, he meets a boy named Joe, who is also in love with the singer-Miss Acacia. Eventually, Jack sets out to find Miss Acacia, despite the warnings of danger.<br /><br />My first main problem is that the love between Miss Acacia and Jack (later on in the book) was all lust. The love was completely physical and full of excitement and giddiness. It didn't feel real or like it was worth risking your life over for. My next big issue, is that I hated Miss Acacia. She was irrational and constantly making Jack feel insecure and jealous. Several of the conflicts in this book were caused by her running off and not fully listening. She was so rash and hysterical. Surely these problems aren't because the book was translated? I really hope not. This book was a disappointment for me and ended completely differently than what I was expecting. Left me feeling empty inside.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1405179132885657665">Bueno, la verdad que se me ha hecho bastante PESADO, hubo momentos en los que me planteaba abandonarlo. En cierto modo me ha decepcionado, sin embargo, el final me ha gustado muchísimo, cómo en las últimas páginas se desarrolla todo tan deprisa, mientras que el resto del libro ha sido TAAAANNN LEEENTTTTTOOOOO.<br/><br/>Mi crítica en mi blog: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://tasteittasteme.blogspot.com/2011/04/la-mecanica-del-corazon.html'>http://tasteittasteme.blogspot.com/20...</a><br/><br/>----<br/><br/>Well, the true is that I thought to give up the book many times. I found it so boring... that I really thought to abandone</span>
  <span id="freeText1405179132885657665" style="display:none">Bueno, la verdad que se me ha hecho bastante PESADO, hubo momentos en los que me planteaba abandonarlo. En cierto modo me ha decepcionado, sin embargo, el final me ha gustado muchísimo, cómo en las últimas páginas se desarrolla todo tan deprisa, mientras que el resto del libro ha sido TAAAANNN LEEENTTTTTOOOOO.<br /><br />Mi crítica en mi blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://tasteittasteme.blogspot.com/2011/04/la-mecanica-del-corazon.html">http://tasteittasteme.blogspot.com/20...</a><br /><br />----<br /><br />Well, the true is that I thought to give up the book many times. I found it so boring... that I really thought to abandone it. In fact, I really hoped much more that I found, but, being honest, last pages were exciting and I really enjoyed them! The story upside down in the last part and it was a surprise after one of the slowest stories I've read until now.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mZ3dXbkVKraKu9oB9wWEehnXkQ+OgJb3h7PB5VPM6IFv7IReQJatnq+TqgOzuOub+xbasgLCWf2h7mqnxIik8Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer10091401151538145691">Mathias Malzieu est une figure phare du rock français avec le groupe Dionysos, pour lequel il écrit, compose et interprète les chansons. Peu enclin à choisir entre sa vocation de chanteur et celle d’auteur, c’est tout naturellement qu’il décide de mêler les deux. Après un recueil de nouvelles, 38 mini westerns, et un roman, Maintenant qu’il fait tout le temps nuit sur toi, il connait un immense su</span>
  <span id="freeText10091401151538145691" style="display:none">Mathias Malzieu est une figure phare du rock français avec le groupe Dionysos, pour lequel il écrit, compose et interprète les chansons. Peu enclin à choisir entre sa vocation de chanteur et celle d’auteur, c’est tout naturellement qu’il décide de mêler les deux. Après un recueil de nouvelles, 38 mini westerns, et un roman, Maintenant qu’il fait tout le temps nuit sur toi, il connait un immense succès populaire avec La Mécanique du cœur (2007), traduit dans 20 pays, et le récit autobiographique, Journal d’un vampire en pyjama (2016), Prix Essai France Télévisions et Grand Prix des Lectrices de Elle.<br /><br />-----<br /><br />Mathias Malzieu is the singer of the French music band Dionysos.<br />He likes to concieve his books like movies, of which he creates an original soundtrack for (Dionysos's latest music records).</span>
  <a data-text-id="10091401151538145691" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    w.attachEvent('onload', go);
  } else {
    w.addEventListener('load', go, false);
  }
}(window, document,
    ['//assets.pinterest.com/js/pinit.js',
     '//apis.google.com/js/plusone.js'
    ]
  ));

//]]>
</script>
